<Rating>4</Rating><review>Good food, had better but it's authentic for sure. Liked the desserts and drink options, I tried them all- I like the milk cakes, but it aint for everyone (im Asian, not picky with my food I prefer it simple, although I never hate on new things, I never let people claim authenticity on foods if its not fact). I am very analytical/specific with my foods.
Had the paneer(cheese) naan. Was shredded cheese, i was expecting melted so it could have been better. Curry and rice portions were perfect, I was full and satisfied with no it is off of one curry and rice. Didn't go spicy with my curry cuz I wanted to actually taste the flavors of the curry, so I cant account for how the spicier currys taste. Shared my dessert and drinks. Im very picky with my food places because there are so many places to try, so I would introduce someone to this place, but personally I would not go back.

This feed store has all your furry and feathered friends needs. Get your dog groomed, buy some baby chicks, get your guinea pigs a new hut. They have friendly staff and there are enough people working that they can stop to discuss the pros and cons of dog food to help you select what you need. They also work to support local businesses like mandarin from a local grower in season and other small pet companies. I like shopping here because it has always been a positive experience and because I feel like my money is staying in my community.</Review>

We lived at Elan for a few years. This would have been a 5 star review, given our large apartment for great value, beautiful gardens surrounding the apartment complex, awesome pools and gym. I see a lot of people complained about the noise, and we indeed heard leaf blowers every day, but I believe that is inevitable in order to keep a property surrounded by trees clean.
The only reason I am giving 4 stars (and I honestly debated giving 3 stars instead), was that a month before our move-out date someone drew a swastika on the elevator door. I sent them an email explaining our concerns and asking what was being done to address the issue. Anthony told me he would forward my email to management, and said they would definitely be in touch regarding the issue. I never heard back from management about this, even after sending a follow-up to Anthony. They also sent an email to the entire community about ‚Äúexterior guidelines‚Äù, as if drawing a swastika on an elevator door had the same impact as keeping shoes outside your door. The incident was not mentioned in that email, or any other email sent to the community. In the month we lived there after the fact, we did not see any additional security camera, and did not see any effort in trying to find out who was responsible for the drawing on the elevator door.
I completely understand that this was a difficult situation to deal with, but after spending wonderful years at Elan, we thought we could hold them to a higher standard. We were wrong.<//text>

<text>I have rented 2 different apartments in Elan for 3.5 years.
+ Safety, I never had something stolen and never saw any cars breaking in in garage as well as on street parking around. Car break-ins is very common case if you unhappy to choose Seely ave to park, but Elan's garage and streets looks quite safe. Neighbors are mostly Indian engineers and their families with good family atmosphere and specific nice appearance.

+ Staff, It's very friendly, I especially thank Dmitry who gave me lot of explanations about rental specifics and guided me when I decided to move from one unit to another.

+- Maintenance. I never had problems with maintenance. All work has been done it short time (usually same day If you come for help to 9am, and next day if you come during the day). Maintenance done for 3 years: Washing machine, fix, Microwave, replacement, Microwave plate, replacement, sink leakage, fixed, AC control unit, replaced, toilet clogging, fixed. Elevator is a curse. It is not working for months, it took about one month for full replacement, then brand new elevator stop working in first week of operation. Hope now it is working. However I think that fixing elevator is not under Elan's control.

+- Living area. Units are very dark, you always need to keep lights on. Also, I heard footsteps of my upper neighbors all the time, including 1,2,3 am. The solution is: you pay extra 100$ to rent and move to top floor unit, which is bright and quiet, that was I did.

-+ Pricing. Pricing itself is reasonable, I mean this is lowest price among competitors in this area. However, price policy could be better. When your 1-year contract is expired you will be treated as fresh new incomer in terms of price for next year. For Elan is seems does not  matter you have lived there for years and always pay in time. So, they are not making any attempts to attract existing good tenants to continue.

0 - amenities. Nothing to say, they are closed last year due to COVID.</text></record></dataset><record>

<review>Located in the heart of Silicon Valley this is a great apartment complex in the South Bay. Living in Elan is truly like living in a resort. With tennis courts, 3 pools and 2 gyms we have all that we need literally right around the corner. We are walking distance from a small strip mall that has a Starbucks, Subway, Pizza, Curry Up Now and a few other restaurants. The apartment complex also allows food trucks to stop by so if you feel like eating out but don't feel like driving you can always walk to the food trucks that come by in the evenings. The apartment management staff are friendly and the maintenance staff is super prompt and friendly as well. Another great feature of this apartment complex is the abundant parking. Unlike other apartments (including our previous apartment) where parking is a problem for guests, we never have that issue as there is plenty of covered and uncovered parking for guests. One drawback of the buildings here are the thin walls which sometimes mean that we can hear our neighbors if they are loud or having a party. All buildings have elevators, shopping cart that you can drag from your car to your unit and what I like most about the design of the buildings is the uncovered passageways leading to and from our apartment. I like that the passages are not covered making the apartment complex look less like a hotel. Another feature that I like is the garbage chute on each floor. Not having to walk to a dumpster to throw my garbage means that I can throw my trash out every night which I really like. The apartments themselves are spacious and well designed. My husband and I currently rent a 1 bedroom 1 bathroom and it's perfect for the two of us. We especially enjoy the open kitchen with plenty of storage space and a separate den(dining room) It's also nice to have a balcony with a huge backyard (for people living on second floor) that allows me to maintain my gardening hobby. The apartment complex has barbeque pits too. In terms of location, Elan is close to 237, 880 and 101 so getting to other parts of the bay is really easy. It's also not too far from the light rail station that connects to downtown San Jose in the south and the Mountain View Caltrain station in the north. All in all a great place to live in the bay area! We have already decided on we'd move from this place only when we buy house of our own.< /review><pics>None</pics>< response>

< text>
We saw at least 20 different apartments before deciding on moving to Elan and we are extremely happy with our choice of the Elan at River Oaks community  and particularly our sunny apartment . The building is really clean, well maintained  and incredibly quiet. The shopping carts on parking lot is a huge bonus. The views from our apartment are spectacular (lakes, fountains, huge trees) it is quiet, very private.

The staff and front desk are extremely friendly and often go out of their way to help. We have not had any major maintenance problems in our apartment the past year, but maintenance requests completed very promptly,  the maintenance staff was efficient in fixing the minor problems we have had.

As former resident I can name all pros and cons:

Pros:
*  stuff is awesome and always have a great attitude
*  beautiful landscape with fountains and lakes (with lovely cute ducks)
*  plenty of  parking spots on two levels
*  shopping carts on parking
*  AC outlet on some parking spots (very easy to vacuum a car)
*  awesome gyms ( two of them are not crowded even in peak hours)
* washer and dryer in unit (actually on your patio! so you won't even hear the noise)
* free tennis lessons
* !!! MOVE - OUT PROCESS was very smooth and friendly. We've got whole our deposit back (except cleaning fee, which is very-very reasonable)

Cons:
- Not the newest building (but still great)
- Club house is accessible 9 am - 6 pm (not 24/7)
- After moving out you'll going to miss this community

Overall fantastic experience! Great place to live!< /text>

<pictures>None</pictures>< Review>
Pros: The management team there was great and very responsive. The amenities are kept in good condition, and the apartments are easy to live in.

Cons: If you're just visiting them, you may get there on a normal day without the infamous Milpitas stink. This was my experience in November 2014, as I had two weeks to relocate to the Bay Area and sought a place near work. The issue, though, is that on specific days one of the worst smells you can imagine travels from the nearby Milpitas dump directly over this space. It is disgusting and miserable to be outside. It will not be mentioned in your visit.

Apart from that, it's not in a walkable part of town. There is a nearby Hobee's and Starbucks that were great to visit, and Paxti's is still walking distance. Without the stink, it's far from a bad place to live, but the smell made it an unlivable situation. For what you're paying in the Bay Area, find a place you won't be disgusted to come home to.< /Review>
